Suttavibhaṅgavaṇṇanā                        hi sati so moceti na rūpaṃ alabhitvā ti rāgūpatthambhādīhipana pañcahi kālo dassito rāgūpatthambhādikālesuhiaṅgajātaṃ kammaniyaṃ hoti yassa kammaniyatte
